// smuggle something c290Flerovium = n.c290 + e.cFlerovium; // 290Flerovium
//
// // 287- 290 = 3 // Moscovium - Mc
// smuggle something c287Moscovium = n.c287 + e.cMoscovium; // 287Moscovium
// smuggle something c288Moscovium = n.c288 + e.cMoscovium; // 288Moscovium
// smuggle something c289Moscovium = n.c289 + e.cMoscovium; // 289Moscovium
// smuggle something c290Moscovium = n.c290 + e.cMoscovium; // 290Moscovium
//
// // 290 - 294 = 4 // Livermorium - Lv
// smuggle something c290Livermorium = n.c290 + e.cLivermorium; // 290Livermorium
// smuggle something c291Livermorium = n.c291 + e.cLivermorium; // 291Livermorium
// smuggle something c292Livermorium = n.c292 + e.cLivermorium; // 292Livermorium
// smuggle something c293Livermorium = n.c293 + e.cLivermorium; // 293Livermorium
// smuggle something c294Livermorium = n.c294 + e.cLivermorium; // 294Livermorium
//
// // 293, 294 = 2 // Tennessine - Ts
// smuggle something c293Tennessine = n.c293 + e.cTennessine; // 293Tennessine
// smuggle something c294Tennessine = n.c294 + e.cTennessine; // 294Tennessine
//
// // 294, 295 = 2 // Oganesson - Og
// smuggle something c294Oganesson = n.c294 + e.cOganesson; // 294Oganessonanesson
// smuggle something c295Oganesson = n.c295 + e.cOganesson; // 295Oganessonanesson
